Not a fan. Their juices aren't real juice, just watered down concentrate. This is the only smoothie place I've ever been to that charges extra for substituting one fruit for another or substituting juice for almond milk. I was planning on coming here every morning, but I can't justify giving such an inflexible business my money. At 20 ounces, their large is smaller than most smoothie places medium size. Not to mention that I was a little grossed out that they don't have paper covers around their straws and they grab the end of your straw with their hand.</Text>

<pictures>None< /pictures><response>None<//response>< Review>
We are not vegetarians or vegans but Chef Lacey makes such delicious non-meat fare we  don't even miss the meat when we eat at Encuentro.  In fact I now usually make a point of skipping anything that is pretending to be a traditionally meaty dish.  Often I really have no idea what to order but it doesn't really matter - I'm seldom disappointed.  Flavor, texture and satisfaction are usually delivered in generous helpings.  Wash it all down with a tasty glass of wine or beer and I'm leaving with a full stomach ready for a nap.

The new location on 2nd at Clay Street has taken a Encuentro to a whole new level - lots more room, no more stuffy temperatures and steamy windows but still a pleasant "organic" atmosphere.   I hope many more will now be able to enjoy Lacey's delicious offerings as a consequence.  San Franciscans - you don't know what you're missing when you wimp out and avoid crossing the bridge to visit.  How lucky we are to have this restaurant slap bang in Oakland and we don't even have to pay a bridge toll to visit it!<//Review>

<rate>4</rate>< Text>
The food here is excellent! Service is reasonably quick and courteous. I found the place to be a bit pricey for what you get, but it is definitely a good option if you are looking for vegetarian, vegan, gluten-free, or all three! Very inventive dishes. Also, don't be afraid of the non-dairy cheeses -- they are delicious! They used to have excellent cornbread, but no longer, unfortunately.

This place does accept reservations, and it was packed for a Wednesday night, so if you have a large-ish party and/or don't like to wait, just call ahead. We arrived half an hour before our assigned time, but they were more than happy to accommodate us.< /Text>

Amazing food--all four of us were raving about what we ate during and after the meal. I'm the only vegetarian among us. Daikon patties, tempeh, farro & veggies, all were big hits. Pot pie was the least favorite (but still very, very good, and we finished it).  Salads were equally tasty. Nice decor and vibe inside. Our server was great--friendly, non-obtrusive, gave us a free mini-dessert (she overheard we were celebrating a birthday). I'm usually not happy paying restaurant prices in the Bay Area--Encuentro is an exception, with a dining experience that made going out a worthwhile pleasure.< /text>

< review>
I dragged my reluctant meat eating boyfriend here. He took one look at the menu and told me to just order since nothing sounded remotely appetizing to him. So I ordered the marinated mushrooms with pecan pate (favorite of the night), stuffed dates with goat cheese, avocado bruschetta, Shephards pie, portobello sandwich, and chocolate cake.

The first thing that came out was the marinated mushrooms. This dish is ridiculous. SO MIND BLOWINGLY GOOD. That pate....I can't even. Every single bite was filled with flavor. Spread it on a piece of cardboard and I would happily eat it. Boyfriend was so shocked how delicious it was that he just kept quiet and focused on the food. The dates were nice and sweet which complimented the goat cheese. The avocado bruschetta was ok, but you can skip it, nothing exceptional.  The shephards pie was hearty. The portobello sandwich WITH the pecan pate was again, amazing. The vegan chocolate cake was surprisingly light and not too dense or sweet.

They were packed when we came on a Wednesday night, so we opted to sit outside.  Plus, it was a bit hot and stuffy in there temperature wise. There's not much of a view (you're essentially sitting on a sidewalk haha) but it was quieter and the weather was nice!

Service was helpful and very friendly. Even though we were outside, we didn't feel like we were neglected at all.<//review>

My wife and I celebrated our one year anniversary at Olivetta and were so happy we did!  We love Marissa and Matt‚Äôs other restaurant, Draycott and thought we‚Äôd see how this compared.  The decor was sexy and the service was fantastic.
